REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,39,426,198902)                                 2213100100003 
           (C,88MITO,,779,1988)                                   2213100100004 
TITLE       Nonstatistical effects observed with 52-Cr + n        2213100100005 
            resonances                                            2213100100006 
AUTHOR     (G.Rohr,R.Shelley,A.Brusegan,F.Poortmans,L.Mewissen)   2213100100007 
INSTITUTE  (2ZZZGEL) G.R., R.S., A.B. Experimental site.          2213100100008 
           (2BLGMOL) F.P., L.M.                                   2213100100009 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL) The 150 MeV Geel Linac, GELINA,        2213100100010 
            operated with a burst width of 4.5 ns and a frequency 2213100100011 
            of 800 Hz, was used for the measurements.             2213100100012 
INC-SOURCE .Uranium target, bombarded with 150 MeV electrons. The 2213100100013 
            neutrons were moderated for the 50 and 200 m trans-   2213100100014 
            mission measurements. In the 60 m capture measurement 2213100100015 
            the beam was collimated to 6.5 cm by copper and lead  2213100100016 
            cylinders.                                            2213100100017 
INC-SPECT  .White neutron source.                                 2213100100018 
METHOD     (TOF,TRN) Time-of-flight techniques, with five neutron 2213100100019 
            flight paths with lengths ranging from 28 to 400 m.   2213100100020 
DETECTOR   .A B4C slab, containing 10-B, being 5 mm thick, was    2213100100021 
            used to detect the neutrons in the 50 m transmission  2213100100022 
            measurements. The 478 keV gamma-ray from neutron cap- 2213100100023 
            ture in 10-B was detected by two 10.2 by 7.6 cm       2213100100024 
           (NAICR)  NaI/Tl/ detectors, situated outside the       2213100100025 
            neutron beam.                                         2213100100026 
           (SCIN ) A 25 mm thick NE 110 plastic scintillator,     2213100100027 
            viewed by four RCA 4516 photomultipliers tubes, was   2213100100028 
            used to detect the neutrons in the 200 and 400 m      2213100100029 
            transmission measurements. In addition, the beam was  2213100100030 
            filtered with  0.37 g/cm2 of uranium.                 2213100100031 
           (BF3) A BF3 detector was used to normalize the         2213100100032 
            sample-in and sample-out runs.                        2213100100033 
           .A 0.4 g/cm2 B4C slab was placed in the beam to absorb 2213100100034 
            low-energy neutrons.                                  2213100100035 
           (SCIN) 10.2 cm diameter by 7.6 cm thick C6D6 liquid    2213100100036 
            scintillators, placed with their axes perpendicular to2213100100037 
            the neutron beam and 180 degrees apart, were used to  2213100100038 
            detect capture gamma-rays in the 60 m capture measure-2213100100039 
            ment. A discriminator level of 150 keV electrons was  2213100100040 
            used.                                                 2213100100041 
           .A B4C slab was used to measure the neutron flux in the2213100100042 
            capture measurements.                                 2213100100043 
           (GLASD) In addition, a Li-glass detector was also used 2213100100044 
            for neutron flux determination.                       2213100100045 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,,SIG) The 478 keV photons associated2213100100046 
            with this /n,a/-reaction was used to determine the    2213100100047 
            absolute neutron flux for the capture measurements.   2213100100048 
SAMPLE     .The samples were in form of chromium oxide, Cr2O3,    2213100100049 
            powder, enriched to a purity of 99.74%. The           2213100100050 
            powder was canned in thin aluminium containers of 8   2213100100051 
            or 3.5 cm diameter with 0.0114 and 0.0593 chromium    2213100100052 
            atoms/barn, respectively. The former was used for the 2213100100053 
            capture and 50 m transmission measurements, while the 2213100100054 
            latter was used for the 200 and 400 m transmission    2213100100055 
            measurement.                                          2213100100056 
CORRECTION .The background in the transmission measurements was   2213100100057 
            determined from black resonance minima using Bi, Na   2213100100058 
            and S filters. The maximum dead-time correction in    2213100100059 
            these measurements was 10%.                           2213100100060 
           .The background in the capture measurements was deter- 2213100100061 
            mined from black resonance minima using Ag, Bi, Co,   2213100100062 
            Na, S and W filters. The neutron flux curves obtained 2213100100063 
            from the B and Li data were corrected for background, 2213100100064 
            detection efficiency, self-screening and multiple     2213100100065 
            scattering effects, were found to agree within 3%     2213100100066 
            in the energy range 1 - 300 keV.                      2213100100067 
ERR-ANALYS .No details given.                                     2213100100068
